  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);

<span id="freeTextContainer432412880122962243">And now we wait...<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383532575ra/6588698.gif' width='250' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/><i>Edit</i><br/><br/><b>5++ badass stars</b><br/><br/>Now THAT, is how you end a book.<br/>I have waited so, so long to finally read the last book in this series, and it surpassed my expectations like I never thought it could. I loved this book so much I can hardly put it into words.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383795573ra/6669256.gif' width='250' height='200' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Aiden and Alex were still the sweetest, most loving couple you can root for in this book which I really hoped would be the case. After what happened in the previous book you would think maybe Aiden would take a step back from Alex and l</span>
  <span id="freeText432412880122962243" style="display:none">And now we wait...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383532575ra/6588698.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br><i>Edit</i><br><br><b>5++ badass stars</b><br><br>Now THAT, is how you end a book.<br>I have waited so, so long to finally read the last book in this series, and it surpassed my expectations like I never thought it could. I loved this book so much I can hardly put it into words.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383795573ra/6669256.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Aiden and Alex were still the sweetest, most loving couple you can root for in this book which I really hoped would be the case. After what happened in the previous book you would think maybe Aiden would take a step back from Alex and let her deal with things more on her own, but no. He stays with her all the way through, supports her, helps her, and loves her more than I've ever seen someone love somebody else. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383795573ra/6669257.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Seth, gods, what a complex man you are. I have had so many mixed feelings towards you, it was hard to keep track of it all. When you were first introduced to us, I freaking loved you all the way, but then you became this power addicted person that made me hate you and want you out of the picture. But now, you come in this book, and be that way? Baby, I can't do nothing else but love you when you're like that.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383795573ra/6669258.gif" width="200" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now the ending. Boy, oh boy, that ending. It's so hard to talk about it while not revealing any spoilers, but man, it has to be said. The ending was the part where I felt a LOT of things. I mean I was a freaking mess. I went from denial, to sadness, to denial all over again. And then I was just so, SO angry at the author. That story could just not end like that. There was no possible way she could do this to us. I was a sobbing mess by then, and I just couldn't wrap my head around what was actually happening. But then, when you think all is wrong, and you hate this book so much you want to throw it at your wall, Jennifer saves the day with the most beautiful, wonderful ending for the most beautiful, and wonderful story there is. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383795464ra/6669240.gif" width="250" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="432412880122962243" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_458638951" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/458638951" />
    <a title="Boyanna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6397486-boyanna"><img alt="Boyanna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567027874p2/6397486.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/458638951?book_show_action=true">Nov 18, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Boyanna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Boyanna" href="/user/show/6397486-boyanna">Boyanna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6397486-boyanna?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer458638951" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2296805392417256573"><a href='http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/2013/11/review-sentinel-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409124216i/10937072._SX540_.png' width='400' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>While reading this book i come to this worthy notions about life:<br/>- teen pregnancy is the bomb!<br/>- man leather pants are having a comeback<br/>- you are considered British if you end every sentence with the word LOVE<br/>- sleeping with a boy in same bed always ends up in sex. Always (ergo)<br/>- romance is dead<br/>- if you don't PDA you are not considered "in love"<br/><i>*(on the side note - the best place for PDA is an official war meeting)</i><br/>- to be considered brilliant you just have to find a room full of morons.<br/>- male</span>
  <span id="freeText2296805392417256573" style="display:none"><a href="http://thebookmaidens.blogspot.com/2013/11/review-sentinel-by-jennifer-l-armentrout.html" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409124216i/10937072._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>While reading this book i come to this worthy notions about life:<br>- teen pregnancy is the bomb!<br>- man leather pants are having a comeback<br>- you are considered British if you end every sentence with the word LOVE<br>- sleeping with a boy in same bed always ends up in sex. Always (ergo)<br>- romance is dead<br>- if you don't PDA you are not considered "in love"<br><i>*(on the side note - the best place for PDA is an official war meeting)</i><br>- to be considered brilliant you just have to find a room full of morons.<br>- male gods (if they exist) never wear upper body clothing<br><i>*(and women gods always wear see-trough gowns)</i><br>- when given the choice between serious talk and sex you should always choose the later<br>- blushing is the only appropriate reaction to a dirty talk (you don't want people thinking you are a slut now, do you?)<br>- 17 year old girls are consider women<br><i>*(also 21 year old boys are consider men).</i> yeah...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383669726ra/6629062.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This series is a story about a 17 year old girl, Greek god descendant, who learns her destiny is to became the God-Killer and battle the War-God to save the world.<br><br>Considering this book is the conclusion of the series one would expect an action packed book with a lot of loos ends to be tied.<br>And yes it does tie loos ends but, by the end you are so bored, you just stop caring. <br><br>The action is practically non existent (with exception of the last 3 chapters and also if you count f-ing... i don't). The characters just struggle through lazy plot, making stupid decisions regarding obvious questions. Some dialogs were repeated through the book, some were left unfinished hanging in the air, or unnecessary dragged through multiple chapters. Also, every third page had some kind of love declaration on it that in stead of making the love more intense and special it just numbed down the feeling making it unworthy and unbelievable.<br><br>But the main thing that bothered me is the same thing that bothered me in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443663449" rel="nofollow noopener">Origin (Lux #4)</a>. The author mixes the New and Young-Adult genres. This book is mislabeled and it makes me a little cheated and a little insulted. <i>(Look at it this way: If the book world was a giant chat room, this book would be the cutesy little-girl picture hiding a sex predator behind it...)</i><br><br>So... The only moment i felt invested in the book was the last <i>(only)</i> Fight Scene. I liked that it was solely Alex and Seth moment of the story (not lovey-dovey moment but equally powerful). Consequently, this was the only book that i developed feelings for Seth, in the previous books he felt like furniture. That and Deacons sense of humor are the only things that makes this a TWO stars book in stead of ONE.<br><br>If you want fighting, snark and a lot of making out without an actual consequence of plot or character development please feel free and read this!<br><br>Over and Out.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1383669726ra/6629063.gif" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>--------------<br><i>*I hid the teasers I posted earlier under spoiler-tag! Just to clarify things: the likes i have so far (118) are for them not for the review.</i><br>Teasers:<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[<i><u>Update 10/25/'13:</u></i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=420215898079978&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1382666016i/6107910.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>------------------<br><i><u>Update 05/10/'13:</u></i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/411924525575782" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser:</a><br>***<br>“Don’t make a pass at Hera,” Hades remarked, moving along. “Zeus doesn’t take kindly to another man making a move on his wife.”<br>That was absolutely ridiculous if you took into consideration the fact Zeus couldn’t keep it in his pants.<br>“Stop staring,” Aiden murmured in my ear, and when I still didn’t look away, he reached around and turned my cheek. “I thought Ixion was located in the lowest part of Tartarus?”<br>I made a face. Only he would know who Ixion was. Aiden had to have been such a goody two shoes in school—the kind of kid who'd raised his hand with the answer to every question. Dork. I loved him.<br>“We took a shortcut, so we’re several levels down.” Hades stopped his horse and swung on large leg down. We'd hit a dead end consisting of dark, slick-looking boulders. “There is another portion of Tartarus that isn’t spoken of in myths.”<br>Seth dismounted with the grace of a feline. “And that’s where we’re heading?”<br>“Yes. We’re going into the Tombs of Tartarus.”<br>“The Tombs of Tartarus?” Aiden repeated, sliding his arm off my waist.<br>Ha! Something he didn’t know. I cast him a look over my shoulder, and then slid off the horse. I stumbled a step when my feet landed. The ground was oddly... soft and buoyant.<br>Hades snorted. “It amazes me that you’re an Apollyon with all your agility.”<br>My mouth opened to fire back, but I squinted. Something was up with the ground. I took a step and my feet sank about an inch in. Aware that Aiden had landed behind me, I bent down and ran my hand over the pale pink ground. It felt like...<br>I jerked my hand back and looked up, horrified. “The ground feels like skin!” <br>A slow smile crept onto Hades’ face. “Zeus got bored with the whole rock and eagle bit.”<br>Rock and eagle bit...? Then it hit me. “Prometheus?”<br>“You’re standing on him,” Hades remarked.<br>My stomach turned. “Oh gods, I think I’m going to vomit.”<br>“Perfect,” the god said.<br>***<br><br>-------------------------<br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=320897654678470&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">This:</a><br><i>"Some people say when life gives you lemons, you make lemonade, but when life gives you one seriously ticked off God gunning for your ass, you prepare for war and you hope for paradise."</i><br>- Alex (Alexandria) Andros<br><br><br><i><u>Update 04/01/'13:</u></i><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/336874156414153" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #1:</a><br>“That’s okay,” Apollo replied, smiling at him in a wholly creepy' hide your kids' kind of way. “When you least expect it, I’m going to turn you into a a pink flower that smells like cat pee.”<br><br><a href="http://www.facebook.com/photo.php?fbid=343474659087436&amp;set=a.286761674758735.51175.285190961582473&amp;type=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #2:</a><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398053i/768833._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i><u>Update 29/04/'13:</u></i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/358015360966699" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #3:</a><br>“Poor Persephone.” He stared down his nose at the god. “That must be hard on her if that’s what gets you off.”<br>I wrinkled my nose. <br>“If her name drips from your forked tongue one more time, I will rip it out,” Hades promised, voice deadly low.<br>Was his tongue really forked?<br>His lips curled up on one side. “What? You don’t like me talking about your wife?” He looked over at the three of us. “Is abduction as a means of marriage still all the rage these days?”<br>Seth arched a brow. <br>“Uh… no,” I said, shaking my head. “It’s really frowned upon.”<br>Hades cheeks deepened in color. “You’re really pushing me.”<br>“I haven’t even begun to push," the Titan replied. <br>Aiden sighed and said under his breath, “Well, this conversation has really digressed.”<br>“Yeah,” I muttered, crossing my arms as I watched the two try to out snark each other. <br>This is going smoothly. Seth’s voice filtered through my thoughts.<br>I kept my eyes on the Titan. He’s not that… bad. I mean, all things considered, right?<br>His answering chuckle tugged at my lips. I sort of like him.<br>Of course.<br><br><i><u>Update 14/07/'13:</u></i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/382124688555766" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #4:</a><br>“Other than the fact I just spewed out two gods like a drunk college chick? I’m feeling fabulous.”<br><br><i><u>Update 06/08/'13:</u></i><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/JenniferLArmentrout/posts/387914941310074" rel="nofollow noopener">Teaser #5:</a><br>Startled, my head jerked up and my eyes met his. They were a furious shade of gunmetal gray, and they were so open. Raw pain flowed from them, and I wanted to look away from that, to take the coward’s way out.<br>“My heart stopped when that damn door closed on me. I could hear you two fighting. I could hear him taunting you, and I could hear him breaking your bones. And there wasn’t a damn thing I could do about it.” He placed his hands on either side of my legs. Tension rippled through the muscles in his arms. “You never should’ve faced something like that alone.” <br>“But you would’ve died.” <br>“And because I love you, I am willing to die to save you from that. Don’t you dare take that decision from me again.” <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_313982421" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/313982421" />
    <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books"><img alt="Kayleigh {K-Books}" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1540157695p2/3996633.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/313982421?book_show_action=true">Apr 17, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kayleigh {K-Books}" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kayleigh {K-Books}" href="/user/show/3996633-kayleigh-k-books">Kayleigh {K-Books}</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3996633-kayleigh-k-books?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer313982421" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7199866807832817740"><a href='http://k-booksxo.blogspot.co.uk/2013/11/sentinel-blog-tour-review-of-sentinel.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sentinel Review on K-Books</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>"And because I love you, I am willing to die to save you from that. Don't you dare take that decision away from me."</i>
</b><br/><br/>Oh My Holy Gods! There are seriously no words to explain just how incredible this book is.<br/><br/>Now before I go any further let me just give you this...<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383939095i/6709896.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Have my JLA Feels box... because dude you are sooooo gonna need them!<br/><br/><i>Sentinel</i> was without a doubt the most heartbreaking yet perfectly beautiful book I have ever read. No really. There are seriously no words.</span>
  <span id="freeText7199866807832817740" style="display:none"><a href="http://k-booksxo.blogspot.co.uk/2013/11/sentinel-blog-tour-review-of-sentinel.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Sentinel Review on K-Books</a><br><br><b>
  <i>"And because I love you, I am willing to die to save you from that. Don't you dare take that decision away from me."</i>
</b><br><br>Oh My Holy Gods! There are seriously no words to explain just how incredible this book is.<br><br>Now before I go any further let me just give you this...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383939095i/6709896.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Have my JLA Feels box... because dude you are sooooo gonna need them!<br><br><i>Sentinel</i> was without a doubt the most heartbreaking yet perfectly beautiful book I have ever read. No really. There are seriously no words. It was amazing. Heartwrenching. Perfect. There are so many emotions I went through while reading this book that that feels box was so needed!<br><br>I have been such a huge fan of Jen's <i>Covenant</i> series since the beginning when <i>Half-Blood</i> was released in 2011. I fell head over heels in love with the storyline and the characters and it has continued to be my favourite series of all time and I am so utterly heartbroken that it has ended. But like they say all good things must come to an end and this ended with a BANG!<br><br>Alex and Aiden have been through it all. But the time has come for it to end. Going to war with the gods is not easy... and you can guarantee that not everyone is going to make it through. But Alex must make the ultimate sacrifice. Can she really get through this not only with her life but with her love by her side?<br><br>Jennifer L Armentrout has once again proven that she is a literary goddess and genius. There is nothing she can write that will turn out bad and <i>Sentinel</i> just proves that. Jen's incredible and addictive writing style pulls you in right from the first page and won't let you go. She draws you in and keeps you guessing right through and when you finally think you know what is going to happen she will throw in the biggest plot twist that will break your heart and have you going "woah did that really just happen?" Throughout <i>Sentinel</i> Jen shocked me to the core and I have come out the otherside of this incredibly heartwrenchingly emotional book in complete awe of her. It's the truth people, Jen is the Queen of everything literary and she is going nowhere but up!<br><br>Alex has always been my favourite YA heroine because... well she is just epically awesome. I adore her and I just kept on loving her more and more throughout the book. Sentinel shows a very different side to Alex, after what happened to her at the end of Apollyon. What happened to her in the past has a definite consequence to her actions in this one but it just made me appreciate and love her even more. She is one strong chica out Alex. I just adore her.<br><br>Oh Aiden, my beautiful, beautiful boy. I adore you and love you and you are just the most incredible, loving, perfect guy ever. Aiden is utter perfection and he just made me fall even more in love with him throughout this final installment of the <i>Covenant</i> series.<br><br>Seth... oh, Seth. Now if you know me at all you will know that I have always from the very first book, hated and despised Seth. Well... brace yourself... I actually liked Seth by the end. I don't love him by any means but he really proved himself in this one and I ended up liking him in the end.<br><br><i>Sentinel</i> is without a doubt the most heartbreaking yet uplifting book I think I have ever read. I couldn't believe what was happening and could barely read as I was crying so much. It's definitely a bittersweet conclusion to the series but at the same time it's completely perfect for this series. Jen proves herself as such a talented author and I just loved every moment. <i>Sentinel</i> was completely addictive and I ended up reading it in one sitting.<br><br><i>The Covenant Series<i> is well and truly my favourite series of all time and is one that I will re-read again and again. I loved every single, heartbreaking yet perfect moment. There couldn't have been a more perfect ending to the series. I am still not ready to let go of these characters and I would love to see a spin-off series with some of the secondary characters. If it happens I will be overjoyed, if it doesn't that's ok too because the series was the best I have ever read.<br><br><i>Sentinel</i>, and the whole <i>Covenant</i> series, was utter perfection. It was addictive, heartwrenching, emotional and uplifting. I can't even put into words all the feelings that I went through. I can't wait to start on one of Jen's new upcoming novels and series. <i>Covenant</i> will leave a big hole in my heart and my life and I don't think anything else can quite fill the hole. Alex, Aiden, Seth and the rest will forever hold a special place in my heart and I will continue to relive this utterly perfect series over and over again forever.<br><br><b><i>"You have my heart, and you have my strength. Make no mistake, I am willing to die for you, but you have to trust that I don't want to leave my side."</i></b></i></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="7199866807832817740" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <span id="freeText10715355599767681893" style="display:none">Omg! Alex, you totally kicked ass. Now kick fate's ass so you AND SETH can live. <br /><br />I wonder what Seth will do in this book because his side...you know...to Alex. He is piiiisssedddd. You just cant mess with a guy's cuddle buddy, man. You may be a God, but he's the Apollyon, asshole.<br /><br />-------------------------------------------<br />This is the last book of this series! Whaaaat?! I knew this day would come. I was begging for it because I just wanted to know what happened and now I'm sad about it. Ha ha ha ha! <br /><br />Though I somewhat enjoyed the Aiden and Alex love affair, I'm ready to let that go. What I'm going to miss, terribly, is the group meetings and Deacon. I love how comical it is just to have all those personalities in the same room. Seth antagonizing everyone, namely Aiden. But Aiden is just so EASY! He's so uptight. It doesn't take anything for him to get under Aiden's skin. I don't understand why! I mean, Aiden has the girl! LOL It's just ridiculous but I love it. I know that he has a lot of shit to make up for in their eyes and that he had to earn back their trust but he was behaving like a freaking saint! FOR THEM. He redeemed himself the second he walked in that gate and <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[got down on his knees. He told her to shoot him in the head and begged her forgiveness! Oh looooorrrddd! And then everything he gives them in the end! They are just GRRRRRRRRRR! <span id="freeTextContainer728196160840165735"><pre>
  <b>"This is everyone's fight.<br/>Because it's everyone's future."</b>
</pre><br/><b>JLA has shattered my heart into pieces <s>again</s></b>💔<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602959613ra/30250722.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Aghhh I knew what was coming, but still... <b>
  <i>it hurts.</i>
</b><br/><br/>Gonna say it right now: If JLA <i>
  <b>ever</b>
</i> repeats an ending like this in any of her future books, I—<br/><br/><b>I don't think I'll be able to survive it.💀</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602968082ra/30251057.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Other than that, the <b>Covenant</b> series will forever hold a special place in my heart. <i>(Although I'm pretty sure I could say that with almost all her books haha)</i><br/><br/>I just love how JLA was able to evolve </span>
  <span id="freeText728196160840165735" style="display:none"><pre>
  <b>"This is everyone's fight.<br>Because it's everyone's future."</b>
</pre><br><b>JLA has shattered my heart into pieces <s>again</s></b>💔<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602959613ra/30250722.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Aghhh I knew what was coming, but still... <b>
  <i>it hurts.</i>
</b><br><br>Gonna say it right now: If JLA <i>
  <b>ever</b>
</i> repeats an ending like this in any of her future books, I—<br><br><b>I don't think I'll be able to survive it.💀</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602968082ra/30251057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Other than that, the <b>Covenant</b> series will forever hold a special place in my heart. <i>(Although I'm pretty sure I could say that with almost all her books haha)</i><br><br>I just love how JLA was able to evolve this whole story in a way I could've <i>
  <b>never</b>
</i> imagined going into this series. <br><br>Who knew it'd go from <b>just any other teenager</b> <i>(at least in this world)</i> dealing with <b>aether-sucking monsters &amp; forbidden love</b> to a more complicated <b>full-out <i>war</i></b> involving the <b>Greek Gods and fate of all realms.</b> <br><br>^Wow, it really sucks being Alex.😓😂<br><br>Now before I go further, I must tell all of you who don't already have this on your tbr <b>TO READ THIS SERIES!!!</b>🥺 <br><br><b>
  <u>🛑There may be mild spoilers in the quotes below!!!🛑</u>
</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Wow.” Deacon elbowed Luke. “This would be awkward if it weren’t so entertaining. It’s like watching our parents—”<br><br>“Shut up, Deacon,” both Aiden and I snapped at the same time.<br><br>“See!” Deacon grinned. “They’re like peas and carrots.”<br><br>Luke turned to him slowly. “Did you just quote Forrest Gump?”</b>
</blockquote><br>Omg I just love <b>Deacon</b> so much.😍😂 He constantly tries to liven up the mood when everyone else is all doom and gloom. Beware of long car rides with Deacon, though xD.<br><b>He. <br>Never. <br>Stops. <br>Talking.</b><br><br>Haha even Marcus couldn't stand it.🤣<br><blockquote>
  <b>I laughed. “I’m not betting against that. On the way here, I thought Marcus was going to strangle him.”<br><br>“I would’ve if he hadn’t fallen asleep,” Marcus said, coming out from behind us. “Or at the very least, I would’ve knocked him out.”</b>
</blockquote><br>^But we still love him.🥰<br><br>The Olympians also made many more appearances during this time, like:<br><br><b>✦ Athena (a.k.a. <i>"The Goddess of Depressing Facts"</i> by Alex), <br><br>✦ Hades (a.k.a. <i>"The God with the British Accent"</i> by Alex), <br><br>✦ Persephone (a.k.a. <i>"The Goddess Who Plays Mario Kart With Caleb"</i> by Alex)<br><br>✦ Artemis (a.k.a. <i>"The Goddess Who Tried to Hit Up on Aiden"</i> by Alex), <br><br>✦ Apollo of course (a.k.a. <i>"The God of Impeccable Timing Who Also Needs a Bell"</i> by Alex).</b> <br><br>There were some others, but those 5 are the only ones I can think of who actually made contact with Alex (and she obviously had amazing encounters with them all hehe xD).<br><blockquote>
  <b>“Gods were like possums.<br><br>You could go your whole life without seeing one, but once you found one of them, you found the whole freaky family.”</b>
</blockquote><br>^She's right. After Apollo, they kept coming right after each other.😆 And it appears to be that the gods have a huge obsession with leather pants because <b>
  <i>"they make it look good."</i>
</b> *sigh* Them and their big egos.🙄😂<br><br>Finally, there's <b>Alex &amp; Aiden</b>😍😍😍 <s>I can't believe I never thought of coming up with a ship name!!! Alaiden? Aldex? No no never mind forget you even saw that.😬</s><br>Those two came a long way from what they once were—especially Alex. I love those two so much.🥺💞 <br><blockquote>
  <b>“He was my strength when I needed him to be, my friend when I needed someone to talk me down, my equal in a world where by law I would always be less than him, and honest to gods, he was the love of my life.”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1602973862ra/30251314.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Apparently, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18809475.The_Return__Titan___1_" title="The Return (Titan, #1) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">The Return</a> is a spin-off of the <b>Covenant series</b> I did <b>
  <i>not</i>
</b> know about that features <b>Seth</b> and some other girl as the MCs.....<br><br>I think I'll probably only read it one day for <b>Alex &amp; Aiden</b>.😏🥺💖<br><br><pre>
  <b>“You know what that means?” I stared into those silver eyes. <br>I had an infinite number of moments like this ahead of me to share with Aiden.<br><br>“They’re going to tell stories about us.”<br><br>Aiden lowered his head, kissing me softly, deeply, and so lovingly that tears pricked my eyes. <br><br>“They already are.”</b>
</pre></span>
  <a data-text-id="728196160840165735" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_754956913" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/754956913" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/754956913?book_show_action=true">Nov 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah">blah</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=die-heroine-die">die-heroine-die</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=blah-romance">blah-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=heroine-is-a-cow">heroine-is-a-cow</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring">boring</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=evul-people-are-evul">evul-people-are-evul</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=boring-main-characters">boring-main-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=cheesy">cheesy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=dead-people">dead-people</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=predictable">predictable</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer754956913" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12451263719417821025"><b>Spoilers</b><br/><br/>A generous two stars instead of one, because I'm just so happy the series has finally come to an end. All I need now is the last <i>Lux</i> installment to come out and then I won't ever have to read another JLA book again. I don't actually have that much of an issue with JLA's writing, it's just that her characters and plots are way too predictable and cheesy for my liking.<br/><br/>-Yea, I'm not a fan of the <i>Covenant</i> series, I'm only reading it because 1. I like to complete any series I've started (even</span>
  <span id="freeText12451263719417821025" style="display:none"><b>Spoilers</b><br /><br />A generous two stars instead of one, because I'm just so happy the series has finally come to an end. All I need now is the last <i>Lux</i> installment to come out and then I won't ever have to read another JLA book again. I don't actually have that much of an issue with JLA's writing, it's just that her characters and plots are way too predictable and cheesy for my liking.<br /><br />-Yea, I'm not a fan of the <i>Covenant</i> series, I'm only reading it because 1. I like to complete any series I've started (even if it's rubbish) and 2. I actually quite enjoy the <i>Covenant</i> world. But it has to be said the <i>Covenant</i> world is more or less exactly the same as the <i>Vampire Academy</i> world but instead of vampires/dhampirs/strigoi, it's all about greek gods/pures/half-bloods/daimons. So yea, I'm not impressed with the copying but since I loved the VA world, it's no surprise that I also enjoy the <i>Covenant</i> one.<br /><br />-What's what: Alex nearly killed by Ares (who's evul and wants war or some BS), Apollo manages to rescue and heal her. Alex whines about everything (as usual), Aiden and Alex act cheesy, Seth returns and acts regretful (fucker), everyone forgets about him being responsible for all the death and destruction. Aiden and Alex declare their undying love for each other even though they're only teenagers, Ares wants everyone at war because of reasons, Alex and the gang need to stop him. Alex has to absorb Seth's powers and become the God Killer/even more of a speshul snowflake so she can kill Ares.<br /><br />-Alex was still as whiny, lame, and irritating as ever. She thought every little thing revolved around her, I was sick of how self-centered and sorry she felt for herself. Yea, she got her arse kicked by Ares but what did she expect? He's an ancient war god and she's not. Why was she so ashamed about that? Even another god couldn't have stopped him so why did she act like she failed? Ugh, she just liked to wallow in self pity. <br />What was most annoying about Alex was her fucked up friendship with Seth. He teamed up with Ares and the bad guys, he caused an apocalypse of sorts, he killed LOADS of people, he didn't care about anyone but his own mummy/daddy issues, he did so many bad things with ease and without feeling any guilt. Yet Alex still acted like Seth wasn't a bad guy. Silly cow.<br /><br />-Why was Alex so sure Seth wasn't playing her when he said he was no longer following Ares? He'd betrayed her once before and she didn't see it coming then, so why not again? There was no evidence that Seth was telling the truth - Alex having a feeling that she could just trust him was bullshit. Okay, Apollo later confirmed Seth was being honest but before then Alex just believed everything he told her. She was so dumb.<br /><br />-Seth didn't redeem himself whatsoever. He was responsible for the deaths of thousands, he wanted to take over the world, kill more people, and make everyone suffer. Him changing his mind and not doing evul things anymore didn't erase all his past evul doings… He was irredeemable. And I was disgusted that Alex and everyone else let him off the hook after a good deed or two. He didn't deserve to be forgiven — he was a vile, murdering, selfish fucker. It makes no difference that he was somewhat influenced by Lucien and Ares, he still had his own mind. He alone decided to be an evul killer. He should have died a horrible death, instead he was made out to be a hero at the end. Ugh.<br /><br />-Aiden was an okay character, he was a bit dull though. His dedication to Alex was sweet but I really didn't understand what he saw in her.<br /><br />-Alex's one liners were still lame.<br /><br />-All the ancient gods acted/talked like teens.<br /><br />-I wish heroines would stop wrapping their arms around their waist whenever they feel bad. I mean, who does that in real life?!<br /><br />-I was glad Alex didn't turn out pregnant. I'm sick of all the teenage heroines getting pregnant at the end of a series.<br /><br />-I didn't expect the weirdness between Apollo and Deacon to be down to them hooking up. That was the only 'twist' I enjoyed.<br /><br />-Alex was always surrounded by guys (Aiden, Seth, Marcus, Apollo, Ares). All the secondary female characters were either in the background and/or played very small or unimportant roles. <br />When Alex thought she was going to die, she had regrets, all of which revolved around the guys in her life. There wasn't one female character she thought of because she didn't give a fuck about making connections with any of them, and the few she did connect with were all dead. Nice.<br /><br />-When Alex was possessed by the evil twin gods she kept banging on about feeling/being different but she didn't actually seem any different from before.<br /><br />-If Perses had been asleep for centuries/millennia then why would he speak in modern day slang?<br /><br />-What was with all the tightening, popping, spasming, and throbbing of jaws? It was as if that was the only way that JLA could convey a character's anger.<br /><br />-I was sick of the repeated mentions of Aiden's eyes. I didn't care what colour they were or what colour they changed to depending on his mood!<br /><br />-All the secondary female characters that were Alex's age ended up dead. It was ridiculous.<br /><br />-I hope there isn't a Seth spin off, he's an awful character.<br /><br />-Ugh, Alex was already a speshul snowflake but she was made into an even bigger one when she turned into a demigod at the end. I would have preferred if she turned fully mortal instead, at least then she wouldn't be as much of a Mary Sue. <br />Oh and Aiden turned into a demigod too. Why couldn't he stay as he was? He could have still been with Alex. Sure, he would have aged but at least then the ending would have been less nauseating.<br /><br />-Dumb quote of the book:<br /><br /><i>Luke blinked, and anger, hurt, and dozen of other violent emotions still infused his cheeks, but he climbed into the back seat with Deacon.</i><br /><br />I didn't know someone's cheeks could convey that much emotion.<br /><br />All in all, it was rubbish. The heroine was a Mary Sue, the hero was a cliched bore, the romance was cheesy, the plot was predictable, the world was decent (but since it was a copy of VA, it doesn't get any points for that), the secondary characters were likeable but were given no depth because everything was all about Alex and her issues. Ugh.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="12451263719417821025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_724757083" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/724757083" />
    <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict"><img alt="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1551124421p2/10717098.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/724757083?book_show_action=true">Sep 21, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carol [Goodreads Addict]" href="/user/show/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict">Carol [Goodreads Addict]</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=paranormal-fantasy">paranormal-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/10717098-carol-goodreads-addict?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer724757083" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13387912249028511441"><a href='http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411340219ra/11217190.gif' alt=' photo tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Some people say when life gives you lemons, you make lemonade. But when life gives you one seriously ticked off god gunning for your ass, you prepare for war and you hope for paradise.” -Alex (Alexandria) Andros</i>
</b><br/><br/>Sentinel is the fifth and final book in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. What can I say about coming to the end of this series? I loved every book, every page and every word. The love story between Alex and Aiden is epic and beautiful. This last book will make you laug</span>
  <span id="freeText13387912249028511441" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411340219ra/11217190.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_n0a7j09qTZ1snlqo0o1_400_zps8201d8f3.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>“Some people say when life gives you lemons, you make lemonade. But when life gives you one seriously ticked off god gunning for your ass, you prepare for war and you hope for paradise.” -Alex (Alexandria) Andros</i>
</b><br><br>Sentinel is the fifth and final book in the Covenant series by Jennifer Armentrout. What can I say about coming to the end of this series? I loved every book, every page and every word. The love story between Alex and Aiden is epic and beautiful. This last book will make you laugh, cry, scream, yell, cheer, cry some more, and sigh, a lot! <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_mqpw23uV5a1r5e3noo1_500_zpse0317c19.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402454904ra/9939981.gif" alt=" photo tumblr_mqpw23uV5a1r5e3noo1_500_zpse0317c19.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>Alex has been put back together after what Ares did to her. She was put back together on the outside, but will never be the same on the inside. She feels like she is broken, never to be the same again. She would have preferred death, wished for death, after what he did to her.<br><br><b>
  <i>The next breath I took scalded my throat. “I think…I think I’m going crazy.”</i>
</b><br><br>Ares is not going to give up. He has Lucian, Seth, and an army of halfs, pures and mortals that are under compulsion. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Ares wants to rule. He thinks it’s time for the gods to reclaim the mortal realm as their own, and I wouldn’t be surprised if there are other gods supporting him.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/greekgod_zps5860acd6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411511894i/11242382.jpg" alt=" photo greekgod_zps5860acd6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Alex and Aiden and their little group are going to gather an Army of Awesomeness to try to defeat Ares. Apollo is on their side. But Ares is the god of war. They need someone to train them and help them with strategy. They are forced to awaken a titan, Perses, for this purpose. But can they trust him or will he even agree to help? And what will they have to trade in exchange? Aiden is forced to make a horrible deal. I was yelling at my e-reader, NO NO NO, he can’t do that!!! <br><br>And then there is Seth, oh Seth! I think in each book of this series my opinion of Seth has changed. The atrocities Seth is responsible for are countless. Will Seth be able to live with what Ares did to Alex? Will he come to his senses?<br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/tumblr_n8i23s1scB1sd2higo1_400_zps28e259e1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411511894i/11242383._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo tumblr_n8i23s1scB1sd2higo1_400_zps28e259e1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And then there is the love story between Alex and Aiden. I have read many of these types of series and I don’t know if I have ever been affected like I was with these two. The weight of the world is on their shoulders, literally. But their only happiness is together. Their strength is each other. The sacrifices they are both forced to make killed me. When Alex was given the opportunity to name something she wanted in exchange for fighting Ares, you won’t believe what she asked for. The depth of Aiden’s love for his Alex, well, “sigh,” there are no words. <br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/sentinel_zps673ba8f2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411511894i/11242384.jpg" alt=" photo sentinel_zps673ba8f2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>So I tried hard not to give anything away. This series is epic…this book is epic!!! Jennifer Armentrout is a rock star! I won’t be forgetting these characters for a very long time. If you are on the fence about reading this series, I say YES YES YES! What are you waiting for. Side note: This book is classified as a YA book but I feel I should say that it really is on the edge between YA and NA. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Agapi mou, you are my everything.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1302.photobucket.com/user/caroldh4/media/elisium_zps5c793adc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411511894i/11242385.jpg" alt=" photo elisium_zps5c793adc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="13387912249028511441" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_740478009" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/740478009" />
    <a title="Marie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6594537-marie"><img alt="Marie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1535710504p2/6594537.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/740478009?book_show_action=true">Oct 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Marie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Marie" href="/user/show/6594537-marie">Marie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=worst-endings">worst-endings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=gods-and-godesses">gods-and-godesses</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=waste-of-time">waste-of-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=disappointing">disappointing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6594537-marie?shelf=what-the-hell">what-the-hell</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer740478009" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11775279221203550479">You know when reading you have an image in your head of a character? Well Taylor Kitsch is the closest to my imaginary Seth. <br/><br/>He.....................<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285221i/7329781.jpg' width='600' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285486i/7329808._SX540_.jpg' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285486i/7329809._SY540_.jpg' height='600' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>IS MINE. <br/><br/>(Whose your imaginary Seth? Comment and add your pics!)<br/><br/><br/>All I wanted from this conclusion was to see Seth happy (and ok. with Alex)<br/><br/>And I don't think I have to tell you with my rating that that is NOT what I got. <br/><br/>I am pissed. <br/><br/>First off yeah, I had a nagging feeling that Seth wasn't going to get his girl. Alex is stupid. <br/>But after everything Se</span>
  <span id="freeText11775279221203550479" style="display:none">You know when reading you have an image in your head of a character? Well Taylor Kitsch is the closest to my imaginary Seth. <br><br>He.....................<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285221i/7329781.jpg" width="600" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285486i/7329808._SX540_.jpg" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1386285486i/7329809._SY540_.jpg" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>IS MINE. <br><br>(Whose your imaginary Seth? Comment and add your pics!)<br><br><br>All I wanted from this conclusion was to see Seth happy (and ok. with Alex)<br><br>And I don't think I have to tell you with my rating that that is NOT what I got. <br><br>I am pissed. <br><br>First off yeah, I had a nagging feeling that Seth wasn't going to get his girl. Alex is stupid. <br>But after everything Seth done to right his wrongs, it still wasn't enough. He gave up everything. Everything!<br>What more did people want from him?<br><br>Yeah he wasn't at his best in the last one, but COME ON, all he wanted was a family, he was manipulated for gods sake in the worse possible way. And he was screwed over. <br>He went through everything Alex felt in that battle -that Seth had no idea of- with Ares.<br>My heart shattered into millions of pieces for him. He always gets shit on. He never has a happy ending. His whole life has been a burden. Left alone. No one to call family. Never gets to love or be loved. Even when he dies he can't find peace because he took Aiden's burden and placed it onto himself. <br><br>I could get over the fact that she picked Aiden but why can't Seth get to be happy? In this book Seth was always there for Alex always looking out for her. But it seemed that there wasn't many friendship scenes or scenes where they just hung out like old times. He didn't even have a friend really in Alex anymore. <br><br>Seth is forever to be alone until he dies and then he becomes Hades pet. His life has never been his own! It has always been hell and that's where he's to stay for all of eternity. <br>Seth was always a good guy even though no-one believed in him, trusted him, not really. <br><br>And what was that short lived pregnancy plot about, well that was pointless! <br><br>This was rushed, considering that all 5 novels have been leading up to this big battle, it was disappointing to say the least, it was short, brief and not much happened. Other than meeting Perses the Titan of war and destruction this book was lacking. <br>There needed to be more Seth and Alex scenes, more action, a bigger battle and of course a HEA for Seth, but I'm never going to get that now. <br><br>Sorry Jen, this book didn't cut it for me. I am never going to be content with that ending, how can I when my favourite character gets to die only to wake up as Hades pet, lord knows how he's going to be treated and what he's going to have to succumb to. It's not right he feels constantly guilty because I don't think he's guilty at all. His past was horrid and he was manipulated and forced into something he believed was the right thing and that Alex was never going to get hurt. And eventually he chose right and even though hard he did the right thing, without his help all would be lost. He was the hero in the end. He shouldn't have been able to take Aiden's place, and it's not right that Alex is ok with Seth's choice. He shouldn't feel so guilty that he felt he owed her his life in order to seek some forgiveness and make up for what happened. <br><br>Everyone's gets a happy ending except him. How is that ever going to be fair? Without him no one would have a happy ending and in exchange for saving everyone he gets forever as a slave. <br>I hate this book. I hate what has become of one of my favourite series. <br>And more time needed to be spent on that battle. Although the Seth/Aiden love triangle was a big part of the series, that was just a subsidiary part of the plot, the battle between the gods? That's what it was all about! And after 5 books it was a tiny battle. The only good part of this book was in fact the twist with the mighty Titan. <br>Oh yeah I am most certainly pissed. Disappointed Jen, disappointed. </span>

          </span>

<div id="review_598733006" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/598733006" />
    <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please"><img alt="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1570038444p2/8422853.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/598733006?book_show_action=true">Apr 24, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ " href="/user/show/8422853-chelsea-peril-please">Chelsea ❤Peril Please❤ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=my-favorite-covers">my-favorite-covers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=unforgettable-male-leads">unforgettable-male-leads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=could-read-over-and-over-again">could-read-over-and-over-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8422853-chelsea-peril-please?shelf=tearjerkers">tearjerkers</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer598733006" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6709952516584824511"><b>5++++++++++ stars</b><br/><br/><b><i>My heart skipped a whole beat, and then sped up in recognition. Ah, I knew that voice. My heart and my soul </i>knew<i> that voice.</i></b><br/><br/>There was a time not all that long ago when I was grappling around trying to find something awesome to read…and I was out of inspiration. I had previously read the Lux series by this very author and had fallen in love, so I thought I’d take a chance and jump-jump into a story I had no clue what the blurb was talking about and give Armentrout another opportu</span>
  <span id="freeText6709952516584824511" style="display:none"><b>5++++++++++ stars</b><br><br><b><i>My heart skipped a whole beat, and then sped up in recognition. Ah, I knew that voice. My heart and my soul </i>knew<i> that voice.</i></b><br><br>There was a time not all that long ago when I was grappling around trying to find something awesome to read…and I was out of inspiration. I had previously read the Lux series by this very author and had fallen in love, so I thought I’d take a chance and jump-jump into a story I had no clue what the blurb was talking about and give Armentrout another opportunity to amaze me-and amaze me she did. <br><br><b>In the darkness, Aiden placed his hand over where mine rested on my stomach, and it stayed that way through the night.</b><br><br>Nine months later and here we are at the end of the Covenant series, and I’m both happy and sad to say goodbye to Aiden, Alex, and Seth-three people who have invaded my heart and haven’t let me go since I picked up the first book. I never would have thought that her Lux series could be surpassed, and I’m not saying it has been, but it’s damn close. A world corrupted by laws that put pure-bloods on a pedestal and halfs in servitude for the smallest mistakes, we are swept into this crazy place where a young girl will strive to rise above these outdated laws and restrictions to fight for the love of her life. Isn’t forbidden love always the best?<br><br><b>As a pure-blood, he was untouchable to me even though I was the Apollyon, and even now he risked everything to be with me. He was my strength when I needed him to be, my friend when I needed someone to talk me down, my equal in a world where by law I would always be less than him, and honest to gods, he was the love of my life.</b><br><br>We have Alex, the half-blood who fell for a pure-blood and knew it could never happen. A girl who was so strong willed she:<br>-Made it on her own with no protection from the covenant<br>-After falling dangerously behind with her training and studies, she came back and rose above the odds-earning a spot at the covenant again.<br>-And ultimately, she became the second Apollyon; an anomaly that almost never happens. But how can there be two….?<br><br><b>I could read everything in his eyes. There was so much pain in them that it broke my heart, but I didn’t understand why.</b><br><br><b>Aiden had to have been such a goody two-shoes in school-the kind of kid who’d raised his hand with the answer to every question. Dork. I loved him.</b><br><br>And then there is Aiden, the pure who fell hard for the half, the pure who offered to train her when no one else would, who pined for that forbidden romance in secret, but wouldn’t be so selfish as to put Alex’s life in danger-because that’s what it is: a matter of life and death. Pushing her away when she needed him most, they both suffer from unnecessary heartbreak that pulls you even deeper into this amazing series and makes you beg for more. He would lay down his life to save her, risk it all with a secret compulsion, battle alongside her only to make sure she lives to see another day-even though he is the one who is really in danger of dying. <br><br><b>”I was selfish in wanting you, knowing what it could mean for you. I was selfish the first time I kissed you, touched you.” The shiver his words brought forth didn’t go unnoticed by him. A dimple appeared. “I was selfish the night I came to your bed when you were at my parents’ house, and I’ve been selfish every day since then. The only time I hadn’t been selfish was when I pushed you away, and that’s the day I regret most.”</b><br><br>Annnddd Seth, the pesky first Apollyon who waltzed into Alex’s life unannounced and charmed his way into her everyday routine. More than once I found myself wishing he would just disappear into oblivion and never come back. He was always a distraction for Alex, someone to challenge her feelings for Aiden, and I never really liked that-but it securely added another intricate layer to these stories that was so desperately needed. Looking back I realize just how much more fun his presence made everything, and I love that he was a part of the journey to where they all are now.<br><br><b>Car keys dangling from his fingertips, Seth passed by us. “If you two can stop making doe-eyes at each other for a few minutes, we’re all ready to go.”<br>Aiden straightened, his gaze narrowing on Seth’s back. “Jealous is an ugly thing.”<br>“So is blind ignorance,” Seth shot back, rounding the front of the Hummer.</b><br><br>A story of power, self-sacrifice, love, loyalty, and strength of will, I couldn’t have loved this final installment more if I tried. Redemption of certain characters and the desperate nature of each person’s willingness to save one another resulted in an even deeper love for this story that was completely unexpected and caused my heart to expand to epic proportions. A race to the finish where no one is safe, even the Apollyons, we watch the story unfold as each character seals their fate, for both good and bad. Sentinel took my breath away more than once with it’s expressive storytelling and ability to make me <b>feel</b>, making for an emotional finish, where nothing can ever be the same, and no one is guaranteed to survive.<br><br><b>It was a beautiful day for war.</b><br><br>There is really no way to express how much I loved this series in one review, because we saw each character grow, mature, and become what they were always destined to be. I laughed, I cried, I <b>bawled</b>, and I frantically wished for the best in the worst of scenarios. I was both surprised and overjoyed with the finale of the Covenant series, and I could even read it again right now. It was just <b>that</b> good. Forever engrained into my soul, I will never forget the joy I felt when I read each installment. For those who haven’t read the series, you are truly missing out on characters that will captivate and compel you, influence you, make you fall in love with them and consume you, and I am so glad I took a chance to find out why each and every one of them is so special-I will always love this series with all my heart and can’t wait to see what Jennifer comes out with next, because I’ll be the first in line, no matter what the blurb entails. <br><br><b>
  <i>And he would wait forever for me, just as I would wait forever and a day for him.</i>
</b><br><br><br><br><i>For more of my reviews visit<br><br><a href="http://starcrossedbookblog.com/" rel="nofollow noopener"><img height="240" width="385" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407869528i/10772466._SX540_.jpg" alt="descriptive text here" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a> </i></span>

<div id="review_553892161" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/553892161" />
    <a title="Summer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/14778159-summer"><img alt="Summer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1574406694p2/14778159.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/553892161?book_show_action=true">Mar 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Summer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Summer" href="/user/show/14778159-summer">Summer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer553892161" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13689155820072178489"><b>1.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Why did I bother? After the shit-fest that was Apollyon, why did I continue with this series?<br/><br/>(Those are strictly rhetorical questions directed at myself. Truth be told, I don’t have the answer to them.)<br/><br/>The fifth and final book in the Covenant series cannot be considered a satisfying “conclusion”. It seemed more like a half-assed attempt, with only Alex and Aiden’s <s>sex</s> relationship given heed, and barely a fleeting glance given to anything else.<br/><br/><b>Why is this book so heavily reliant on roma</b></span>
  <span id="freeText13689155820072178489" style="display:none"><b>1.5 stars</b><br><br>Why did I bother? After the shit-fest that was Apollyon, why did I continue with this series?<br><br>(Those are strictly rhetorical questions directed at myself. Truth be told, I don’t have the answer to them.)<br><br>The fifth and final book in the Covenant series cannot be considered a satisfying “conclusion”. It seemed more like a half-assed attempt, with only Alex and Aiden’s <s>sex</s> relationship given heed, and barely a fleeting glance given to anything else.<br><br><b>Why is this book so heavily reliant on romance?</b> I really shouldn't be surprised, considering how her other novels that I've read of late were. And it’s not even enjoyable romance; it’s downright cheesy and agonizing to read about.<br><br>I can’t believe I hadn't noticed this from the start, but Aiden was too damn perfect. He is the personification of every teenage girl’s lust. If you juxtapose him with other “hawt” love interests of the YA genre, their almost-nonexistent personalities would be practically indistinguishable. <br><br>Alex was even worse. Like I said, I can’t believe I never noticed how stupid these characters are. Here is a quote regarding one of their million make-out sessions: <br><blockquote>
  <i>”There was probably a lot to do today.” </i>
</blockquote> <br>No shit.<br><blockquote>
  <i>”Some would also say there were a lot more important things we could be doing at this very moment.”</i>
</blockquote><br>Actually, that’s exactly what I’m saying.<br> <blockquote>
  <i>”I would argue against this point voraciously, because there was nothing more important than this.” </i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1384142243ra/6790356.gif" width="251" height="161" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Also, what is it with the mention of Aiden’s gray to silver change in eye color? I wish I had counted the amount of times Alex commented on how his “eyes changed from gray to silver”. <br><br>The action scenes were okayish, and relatively few and far between. I actually appreciated the last fighting scene, saving me from <i>completely</i> hating this book.<br><br>Seth was the only character I liked. He grew considerably from when we first met him, and although the author didn’t give him the attention he deserved, I quite liked the scenes he was in.<br><br>THE CONCLUSION WAS HORRIBLE. HORRIBLY-HORRIBLE. This is not a conclusion to the series; instead of wrapping things up, we get a corny/selfish HEA that is pretty much written in favor of Alex. Who was forced to suffer? Seth. The character who is supposed to be the most selfish, is now the most selfless. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[On a side note, how come when Olivia died she was barely given any attention, but when Alex died, shit went crazy? Tut tut. I sense an author playing favorites here. *looks pointedly at Jennifer Armentrout* <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Something that pissed me off was why pregnancy was brought up in the first place, and on top of that, <i>encouraged</i>. Hold up, let me go watch the latest episode of 16 and Pregnant so I could be even more motivated to become a teen mom.<br><br>In case you’re deliberating on reading this, let me give you a run-down of what occurred in the first, oh, two-thirds of the novel: (no spoilers, of course)<br><br>1. Alex and Aiden making out<br>2. Alex lusting over Aiden’s magically changing gray-silver eyes<br>3. Sexxx<br>4. Yelling at Seth/Apollo/whoever<br>5. More kissing at inappropriate times<br>6. More lusting<br>7. Everyone (Aiden) talking about how speshul Alex is<br>8. More sexxxx<br><br>No, seriously. The book ends on a sex scene.<br><br>One would think Ms. Armentrout got mixed up between her young adult and new adult novels.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="13689155820072178489" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1213186548" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1213186548" />
    <a title="Hillary" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/18999155-hillary"><img alt="Hillary" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1601752862p2/18999155.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1213186548?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Hillary" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Hillary" href="/user/show/18999155-hillary">Hillary</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/18999155-hillary?shelf=greek-mythology">greek-mythology</a>,

          </div>
