        <div class="reviewText stacked">
                  <em>
                    This review has been hidden because it contains spoilers. To view it,
                    <a href="#" onclick="Effect.toggle(&#39;reviewTextContainer1213186548&#39;); return false;">click here.</a>
                  </em>
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1213186548" class="readable"
                    style="display:none"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10066722427410586096"><u>Reread update</u><br/>I already knew how everything was going to end but damn I still did cry a river. Now my face is all sticky.<br/><br/>**********<br/><br/>I'm kinda shocked. I need to go hide in a corner and awful cry. Bye.<br/><br/>Damn you book! DAMN YOU.<br/><br/>You know the feeling when you want to throw the book into a wall and then step on it, insult it while crying like a baby and at the same time you want to hug, squeeze it to death because it was just so damn perfect? <br/>...<br/>That's what I'm feeling now.<br/>My mind has gone to Crazy Town </span>
  <span id="freeText10066722427410586096" style="display:none"><u>Reread update</u><br />I already knew how everything was going to end but damn I still did cry a river. Now my face is all sticky.<br /><br />**********<br /><br />I'm kinda shocked. I need to go hide in a corner and awful cry. Bye.<br /><br />Damn you book! DAMN YOU.<br /><br />You know the feeling when you want to throw the book into a wall and then step on it, insult it while crying like a baby and at the same time you want to hug, squeeze it to death because it was just so damn perfect? <br />...<br />That's what I'm feeling now.<br />My mind has gone to Crazy Town and won't be back very soon.<br /><br />I loved everything of this book, but the ending was so bittersweet and I think I need some time to process and accept it. It doesn't help that the series has ended.<br /><br />********<br /><br /><i>It was a beautiful day for a war.</i><br /><br />And <b>what</b> a war.<br />This last book is all about preparation for war. It's fast-paced and also covers a so little time. Not gonna lie, I wanted more, but I also think that this was the perfect ending for a magnificent series.<br />It's one of my favorites. It gave me all the possible imaginable feels on Earth, and I'll never stop thanking JLA for creating it.<br />The thing is… I’m not ready to let Aiden and Alex go. They conquered a really big part of my heart, and this is something that almost never happens to me. I can fall in love with a book and rant about it for decades, but it’s different when the characters and the story enter my heart.<br />Alex, Aiden, Seth, Deacon, Marcus, Apollo and everyone… I will miss them terribly (except for Seth because, you know, JLA is wonderful and decided to write a series about him!).<br /><br /><i>“You’ve never been more beautiful to me than you are right now.”</i><br /><br /> This IS love. Give me an Aiden who loves me unconditionally. He’s SO PERFECT, but also has his flaws, but he’s SO PEFECT.<br /><br /><i>As we walked toward the dean's office, he reached over, trailing his fingers along my arm. "Do they still react when I touch you?"<br />Heat crawled through my veins, and I nodded. The marks had followed the path of his touch. "Yeah, they still like you."<br />One side of his lips curled up, and a look of male pride crossed his face. I shook my head. Boys.</i><br /><br />And honestly, every man in this series is perfect but has flaws and is real. Take Seth: he’s done terrible things, but took a step back when he understood what he really was doing. At the end he’s consumed by guilt and does incredible things for Aiden and Alex. Yeah, you heard me: for AIDEN. The two couldn’t stay in the same room for two seconds without punching and insulting each other, and THEN this happens. I have no words. I already loved him so much, but now my love for him has reached the next level. Marry me?<br />Also his breakdown when he discovered that Alex had to die… he loves her so much. I wanted to bear hug him.<br /><br />The things I love the most about this series apart from the boys…?<br /><br /><u>The fact</u> that Alex is so badass. Girl power, yasss! (I talk about this in every single review, I know, but I don’t care. I just love Alex.)<br /><i>He stared at us like he wanted to rip my hand out of Aiden’s and then take a day’s worth of time to explain why we shouldn’t be holding hands.<br />My eyes narrowed on him as I raised my free hand and scratched the bridge of my nose… with my middle finger.</i><br />Don’t mess with Alex, little boys.<br /><br /><u>The fact</u> that everything is funny, even in the worst moments. At the beginning of the book Alex was depressed (not her fault) but either way I laughed. SO. MUCH. She’s funny even when she’s depressed; I think she deserves a crown. <br />Not to mention the other characters. Apollo, WTH? He always interrupts such great moments between Alex and Aiden, and he does it on purpose throughout the entire series (even when he wasn't a god); but in this book he reaches the limit. I can’t think about it without bursting into uncontrolled laughs. Really Apollo, reallyyy?<br />Besides, have Deacon and Apollo actually ….????? Gods AHAHAHH<br /><i>"Oh! You're one to talk!" I whirled on Apollo. "Seriously? If I was to Google 'irresponsible sexual activity', it would be your picture staring back at me!"<br />Apollo made a face at me—actually made a face at me like he was ten years old or something."</i> <br />And Marcus? Poor uncle, he wants to separate Alex and Aiden, but man, it’s too late hahaha.<br /><br /><u>The fact</u> that everybody goes through major character growth. It's all so well developed that you don't notice it until you read some quotes or think about the previous books. Then it strikes you.<br /><br /><u>The fact</u> that mythology is used in such an awesome way. Indeed, not only it’s realistically portrayed, but is also elaborated to create something new, to attach it in a perfect way to the world-building of the series. In this way Alex’s story really could be considered as a new Greek myth. <br /><br />So. This is a sad goodbye, but hey. Alex and Aiden, you followed me for almost a whole year, so you won’t get rid of me that easily. Wait for me until my first reread.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10066722427410586096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer12064450273769633734">This book is a major heartbreak and the ending is a never-ending plot twist. <br/><br/>So much action. So many things happening in this book. Fights. Battles. Gods. This was mind-blowing. The best conclusion to this series that we could ever get. <br/><br/>All I wanted was for Alex and Aiden to be together because this kind of love deserves to keep on thriving on and on until the end of time. I'm grateful to Seth as much as I do not like him, I know he loves Alex and he, technically, does something awe-inspiring fo</span>
  <span id="freeText12064450273769633734" style="display:none">This book is a major heartbreak and the ending is a never-ending plot twist. <br /><br />So much action. So many things happening in this book. Fights. Battles. Gods. This was mind-blowing. The best conclusion to this series that we could ever get. <br /><br />All I wanted was for Alex and Aiden to be together because this kind of love deserves to keep on thriving on and on until the end of time. I'm grateful to Seth as much as I do not like him, I know he loves Alex and he, technically, does something awe-inspiring for Alex and well, that made me love him. There!<br /><br />I am not the type who loves the get-married-have-babies happy ending thing. Hell, I sometimes prefer tragedy. But this book made me cry at first because, yes, I admit that for this book series I wanted a happy ending due to the fact that Alex and Aiden's love makes me feel too much, but then I was so super-extra-duper happy and extremely confused and perhaps a little bit of awed because it was such an amazing plot to bring the two leading characters together and creating the perfect happy ending but also achieving an out of the ordinary happy ending. <br /><br />I would have given this a 4/5 because I felt like the fight with Ares lasted only for a chapter, I was expecting something much bigger that would affect everyone on a much bigger scale and of course be a little more long-lasting. But, eventually, I gave it a 5/5 because of the unpredictable ending and the fact that I'm still sobbing because of Alex and Aiden. I have told this before but these two are the epitome of "two people in love will eventually be together no matter what". <br /><br />A round of applause for Jennifer L. Armentrout because let's not kid ourselves she is awesome and she knows how to compose an incredible world and create characters that you fall in love with. </span>

<div id="review_1354686826" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1354686826" />
    <a title="Pilar ☽" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/26734182-pilar"><img alt="Pilar ☽" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1441771468p2/26734182.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1354686826?book_show_action=true">Aug 04, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Pilar ☽" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Pilar ☽" href="/user/show/26734182-pilar">Pilar ☽</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=laugh-out-loud">laugh-out-loud</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=love-the-heroine">love-the-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=tears-everywhere">tears-everywhere</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=well-hello-there-mr">well-hello-there-mr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=you-are-a-jerk-but-ily">you-are-a-jerk-but-ily</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=bad-bad-boy">bad-bad-boy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=best-of-the-best">best-of-the-best</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/26734182-pilar?shelf=fabulous-characters">fabulous-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1354686826" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer932452887944672299"><b>1000000000 STARS!!!!</b> <i>(FULL REVIEW OF THE WHOLE SERIES)</i> <br/><br/><i>
  <b>“Some people say when life gives you lemons, you make lemonade. But when life gives you one seriously ticked off god gunning for your ass, you prepare for war and you hope for paradise.” </b>
</i><br/><br/>Oh, my God<i>s</i> and Holy Daimon Babies! This series, I have no words, JLA left me utterly amazed again! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381683173ra/5184886.gif' width='400' height='167' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I have so many feelings right now. I'm soooo, so extremely happy because of that perfect ending but sad at the same time because it's over. <br/><br/>I literally lo</span>
  <span id="freeText932452887944672299" style="display:none"><b>1000000000 STARS!!!!</b> <i>(FULL REVIEW OF THE WHOLE SERIES)</i> <br><br><i>
  <b>“Some people say when life gives you lemons, you make lemonade. But when life gives you one seriously ticked off god gunning for your ass, you prepare for war and you hope for paradise.” </b>
</i><br><br>Oh, my God<i>s</i> and Holy Daimon Babies! This series, I have no words, JLA left me utterly amazed again! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381683173ra/5184886.gif" width="400" height="167" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I have so many feelings right now. I'm soooo, so extremely happy because of that perfect ending but sad at the same time because it's over. <br><br>I literally loved everything about the <i>Covenant</i> series. I was captivated by every chapter and thanks to Jennifer's writing style and creative mind I was completely absorbed in the story. I don't know how she does it, everytime I read a paranormal book written by her I found myself loving every little thing about it. The world building of this story was incredible, I used to read greek mythology when I was young so it brought back old memories. Another thing I really enjoy about JLA writting is that she always makes me fall in love with every character... <br><br>You know that feeling when you start a book and you instantly know that you will love and connect easily with the main character? Well, that's how I always feel when I choose to read a JLA (paranormal) book. I got that exact feeling when I picked up "Daimon" and started reading <b>Alexandria Andros'</b> POV. The best way to describe her is as a kickass and badass heroine. I asbolutely loved her character, she was so strong, independent and with the best sense of humor, I literally found myself laughing most of the time. I'm so happy that she finally got her happy ending, she truly deserved it. <br><br><b>
  <i>I wouldn't give up being a Sentinel for the world. Or being the Apollyon. I rock."<br>"Wow. You're so humble.” </i>
</b><br><br>Now taling about our boy Aiden, I had a hard time loving him (like everyone else) at the beginning because I was 100% team Seth and I found his moments with Alex boring (I needed some action for christ's sake) but since book 2.5 I finally got those "marry me" feelings... He was a sweetheart and my god, I loved his "Alex, lets make babies" side! <br><br><b>
  <i>“Agapi mou, you are my everything.” </i>
</b><br><br>And of course, let's not forget of the supporting cast. Deacon (my fave, tHANK YOU JLA FOR NOT KILLING HIM), Luke, Marcus, Apollo, Lea, Olivia, Caleb, Solos etc, I lOVE THEM ALL DEARLY. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I feel like there should have been more Deacon/Luke/Apollo moments... Am I the only one? There should have been some lover boysssss drama!  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Oh and my Sethie, I'm not going to say much about him here because I will pour out my heart when I write "The Return" review. Heh, needless to say that he was also one of my faves. <b> #TeamSethAllTheWay </b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1439411524ra/15833528.gif" width="400" height="217" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ugh, I hate to say goodbye to an amazing series... I don't know why I haven't read this before but I'm glad I did it because it was a wonderfull journey, full of laughs, kickass moments, passion, love, drama, family and friendship. These books really had it all! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380416234ra/821963.gif" width="400" height="173" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now it's time to move on to Seth's book, I'm so freaking excited I can't wait!!! <br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_750474312" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/750474312" />
    <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library"><img alt="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1350750103p2/4551536.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/750474312?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Maja (The Nocturnal Library)" href="/user/show/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library">Maja (The Nocturnal Library)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=failed-to-impress">failed-to-impress</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=i-have-superpowers">i-have-superpowers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=my-flat-army">my-flat-army</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=just-another-book-crush">just-another-book-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4551536-maja-the-nocturnal-library?shelf=reviewed-in-2013">reviewed-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer750474312" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6150348661616251795">Five books filled with mythology and action; countless painful, almost heartbreaking moments; hundreds and hundreds of pages of deliciously hot romance… and now, we have finally reached the conclusion. The time has come to say goodbye to Alex, Aiden, Seth, Marcus and everyone else. Was this finale everything I’d hoped for? Well, no. But in the end, it made me feel peaceful and calm, happy with how we left the characters we’ve grown so attached to. <br/><br/>And make no mistake, my feelings for the charact</span>
  <span id="freeText6150348661616251795" style="display:none">Five books filled with mythology and action; countless painful, almost heartbreaking moments; hundreds and hundreds of pages of deliciously hot romance… and now, we have finally reached the conclusion. The time has come to say goodbye to Alex, Aiden, Seth, Marcus and everyone else. Was this finale everything I’d hoped for? Well, no. But in the end, it made me feel peaceful and calm, happy with how we left the characters we’ve grown so attached to. <br><br>And make no mistake, my feelings for the characters are exactly what kept me reading through all the rough patches, plagiarism, occasional inconsistencies and the intolerable love triangle in those first few books. There were some horrible moments, yes, but if Armentrout knows anything, it’s how to keep her readers happy. Fan service is always at the very top of her list, and there was never any chance of her repeating the Veronica Roth fiasco. <br><br>In Sentinel, all of her qualities are even more enhanced. There are a lot of great moments fans will appreciate greatly, a lot of quality time spent with the characters, some truly magnificent action scenes (though not as many as one would expect), and of course, the romance is as swoon-worthy as ever, if not more. <br><br>Once you remove the emotional factor, however, and look at Sentinel objectively, all the flaws become painfully obvious. For a final installment, Sentinel was pretty uneventful around the middle. In fact, not much happened until that very last part, and while I admit that those last few pages made me reach for my tissues, the emotional impact wasn’t as strong as it could have been. <br><br>Armentrout’s writing is nothing to write home about, it never was, but in Sentinel, she made quite a few errors, more so than usual. I resent sloppiness – call it a personal flaw, if you will – and sloppiness towards language is the absolute worst in my eyes. When a Titan who’s been asleep and imprisoned for millennia wakes up and starts talking in modern colloquialisms, I consider it to be the result of sloppiness on the author’s side. How he managed to learn expressions like ‘all the rage’ while sleeping in the Underworld is beyond me, but he certainly started uttering them the second he opened his eyes. That is the kind of thing that can ruin a book in a heartbeat, an author not caring enough or not having enough skill to ensure appropriate language for his or her characters. <br><br>Looking back, there are so many things I could say about this series, and I did, in fact, express them all in my reviews. I don’t know that I’d go out of my way to recommend Covenant to someone since there are so many other series out there that for which I don’t have to make excuses, but I still had a lot of fun reading these five books. It is a fact that cannot, and should not, be ignored.<br><br><br><a href="http://www.thenocturnallibrary.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380226536i/681142.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6150348661616251795" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_414721798" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Tina" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6383594-tina"><img alt="Tina" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1371867364p2/6383594.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/414721798?book_show_action=true">Sep 14, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tina" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tina" href="/user/show/6383594-tina">Tina</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer414721798" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer13517002662396488278">5 Stars!<br/><br/>I'M BIASED. I'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASED. I'm a huge JLA fan and a huge fan of this series so is it really a surprise I consider this book 5 stars worthy? I'll keep it short since I personally find it difficult to write long reviews for a book that's later in the series, so let me put it simply:<br/><br/><i>If you're been a huge fan since book 1: <b>you'll LOVE this final book (if not at least like it).</b><br/>If you're been on the fence or haven't been a huge fan: this book probably won't do m</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13517002662396488278" style="display:none">5 Stars!<br /><br />I'M BIASED. I'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASEDI'MBIASED. I'm a huge JLA fan and a huge fan of this series so is it really a surprise I consider this book 5 stars worthy? I'll keep it short since I personally find it difficult to write long reviews for a book that's later in the series, so let me put it simply:<br /><br /><i>If you're been a huge fan since book 1: <b>you'll LOVE this final book (if not at least like it).</b><br />If you're been on the fence or haven't been a huge fan: this book probably won't do much for you.</i><br /><br /><br /><i>Sentinel</i> is just as (if not more) hilarious than the previous 4 books, has a tiny fraction less romance (considering Ares is still causing mayhem, it's understandable) though it does get pretty romantic once the love moments pop up, and there's a fair amount of action. The only minor complaint I have is that the big battle wasn't as long as I thought it'd be. Don't get me wrong, it was great (definitely a lot of action) but I was just expecting the scene to last a tiny bit longer than it did. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Also, am I the only one who's sad that we didn't get to hear from Olivia again? ;_; She's not like my most favorite character, but I do like her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />Nonetheless, I still enjoyed the final book and am sad to see it all come to an end. Thank you Ms. Armentrout for being such a wonderful and dedicated writer! I absolutely can't wait to see whatever work you come out with next!</span>
  <a data-text-id="13517002662396488278" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39317215-majo?shelf=4-stars">4-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/39317215-majo?shelf=fav-villain">fav-villain</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1873755296" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11343181171149743844"><i>4,5 stars</i> Warning: Minor Spoilers ahead.<br/><br/>This is the perfect ending to this perfect series. I love the plot, and I love how everything is tied up at the end. There is a lot of action in this book and I enjoyed every second of it. Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius. I enjoy everything she writes. <br/><br/>I love all the characters: Not just the protagonists, but also the different Gods, especially Apollo. I love Apollo so much, and I laughed every time he appeared in an <i>Alex-&-Aiden-sexy-time</i> situation. I </span>
  <span id="freeText11343181171149743844" style="display:none"><i>4,5 stars</i> Warning: Minor Spoilers ahead.<br /><br />This is the perfect ending to this perfect series. I love the plot, and I love how everything is tied up at the end. There is a lot of action in this book and I enjoyed every second of it. Jennifer L. Armentrout is a genius. I enjoy everything she writes. <br /><br />I love all the characters: Not just the protagonists, but also the different Gods, especially Apollo. I love Apollo so much, and I laughed every time he appeared in an <i>Alex-&amp;-Aiden-sexy-time</i> situation. I love Caleb and Olivia, and Solos, and obviously Deacon and Luke. I ship them so much. <br /><br />Now, Aiden and Alex. They were freaking PERFECT in this book. <br /><b>
  <i>"Agapi mou, you are my everything."</i>
</b> <br />I love how things turned out for them. They're just so amazing together and I <i>lovelovelove </i>how they can overcome everything. I enjoy so much of stories with "forbidden love". <b>And their love story, since book one, was BEAUTIFUL</b>. How they start to train together, and feel attracted to each other, but don't do anything about it because the relationship between pures and half-bloods is not allowed. Scenes like the one in the zoo, or the one when they were in Aiden's house and he plays the guitar for her, or when they have to go to the underworld together. To read about how their love grows up and make both of them stronger was so fucking emotional. They are one of my favorite couples of all times. <br /><br />And last but not least, Seth. I have to be honest: I loved Seth in the first two books. Then I started to hate him in book three, and by the fourth book I just couldn't stand him. All I wanted to do was to punch him. But in this book, IN THIS BOOK, he redeems himself and I can't help but loving him with everything that I am. The sacrifice he made for Alex and Aiden melted my heart. And I can't wait to read the <i>Titan</i> series to fangirl over him once again.</span>

          </span>

  <span id="freeText16069906625450175259" style="display:none">My Alex and Aiden:<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383677217i/6630598.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>I was sad, yet excited to start this final instalment. Once again, Jennifer L. Aremntrout managed to write exciting and thrilling story, full of Greek myths coming alive in our contemporary world. This may not be my favourite part of series, but I was still able to enjoy it a lot!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1383570840i/6598629._SX540_.png" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you for whatever reason have not read this series yet, you should do so now. If not for action-packed, gut-wrenching storyline, than read it because of <b>Aiden St. Deplhi</b>. I am not sure if I have ever read about more devoted, loyal and loving male character before. He is just perfect!<br><br>I cannot really talk about this book without giving spoilers. So all I am going to say is that even though I enjoyed this book and was ok with ending, <b>I did not love it</b>. So why not higher rating? Firstly, I felt like climax was in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9897164.Apollyon__Covenant___4_" title="Apollyon (Covenant, #4) by Jennifer L. Armentrout" rel="nofollow noopener">Apollyon</a> and this was just aftermath. Story was a little bit repetitive, nothing completely new or shocking has happened in this book. Also, I know that this was Alex's and Aiden's story, but after so much time I had spent with this series, there was no proper goodbye with supporting characters. Everything ended so abruptly. <br><br><b>I highly recommend this series to all YA paranormal readers! It is definitely my favourite series when it comes to Greek mythology!!!</b><br><br>MORE REVIEWS ON MY BLOG <a href="http://readingismybreathing.blogspot.cz/" rel="nofollow noopener">

  <span id="freeText2378065736453315440" style="display:none">***Mini-spoilers alert!***<br />Oh my Gods! This last book of the series was amazing! <div id="review_1803727211" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1803727211" />
    <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu"><img alt="Ramona Popescu " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594649997p2/33526516.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1803727211?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ramona Popescu " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ramona Popescu " href="/user/show/33526516-ramona-popescu">Ramona Popescu </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-this-series">love-this-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=fantasy-paranormal">fantasy-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=funny-as-hell">funny-as-hell</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=something-new">something-new</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=hot-romance">hot-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=man-crush">man-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=love-and-action">love-and-action</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/33526516-ramona-popescu?shelf=sweet-as-sugar">sweet-as-sugar</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1803727211" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6221245541589997600">Finally the series is complet and I am blown away! I am not surprised in the least, because I loved everything about it from second 1 until the end. This is definitely one of my favorite series and I want to kiss myself for taking the decision to read it and to not have breaks them, because they are a fully and amazing adventure. You must read them continuously, because the plot is very complex and if you change the book, you might forget some very interesting aspects. <br/><br/>My point is that I adored </span>
  <span id="freeText6221245541589997600" style="display:none">Finally the series is complet and I am blown away! I am not surprised in the least, because I loved everything about it from second 1 until the end. This is definitely one of my favorite series and I want to kiss myself for taking the decision to read it and to not have breaks them, because they are a fully and amazing adventure. You must read them continuously, because the plot is very complex and if you change the book, you might forget some very interesting aspects. <br><br>My point is that I adored this series and the impact it had upon me was huge. Not wanting to have a reading slump, I will dive right into another book, but I will think about "The Covenant" for a long time.<br><br>So, Alex is the freaking Apollyon with a freaking mission. She has to transfer Seth's power into her, become the God Killer, kill the evil God and after that, face the consequences. The book was extremely dynamic, with a lot of heavy moments, but also emotional and steamy ones. You never know where the story will progress, how it is going to turn out and Jennifer killed me in "Sentinel" because the last 5 % of the book were painful, full of emotions and unpredictability. I KNOW I forgot to breathe at some point. And not to spoil something, but Seth will be actively involved in this book, for those who love him and wished a different outcome for him. There is still hope, Alex was right:) <br><br>Alex was soooooo bad ass and I will never forget her as a heroine. She was unique, her style, her courage and her spirit were amazing, a true example for all of us. I don't want to enter in many details about Aiden, because he easily made the Top Book Boyfriends of all time and maybe the revelation of this year. This couple was amazing, the intensity between them was OFF THE CHARTS and you could feel their love, their connection, their meaning to be together. Even the scenes between them that were not extremely explicit, left you gasping and blushing, because they were so good and full of energy. I could spend hours talking about them and the series, but seriously, read it and you will love it as much as I did.<br><br>The final chapter was different and from my POV very original and not as I have imagined it. I know it will leave you in a 50-50 position, not knowing which side to choose... love it or be confused? I chose both of them, because after the various adventures, twists and problems this characters had to face, you couldn't believe the ending will bring total closure right? You know the dots from "The End...", well, they describe perfectly this book, like a "To Be Continued", because out characters will be with us soon. <br><br>Believe me, it is very hard to cope with the idea that this series has ended.. I will miss them terribly, but for those who want to read more about this amazing characters, read "The Titans"series, a spin-off, that centers Seth and Apollo's daughter, Jodie. Plus, you will have some awesome surprises in stored.<br><br><br>5 stars!!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1479123324i/21149668._SX540_.png" width="500" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more reviews please check <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com">https://readwithloveblog.wordpress.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="6221245541589997600" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=best-leading-lady">best-leading-lady</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=healing">healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=audioread">audioread</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=forbidden-love">forbidden-love</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1074713340" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14370330969681367636"> <b>"It's time!"</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422854941i/13554782.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Sentinel is the fifth and final book of the Covenant series. Everything that has transpired in the past four books has been leading to this moment! Sentinel did not disappoint.<br/><br/>Alex has been battling her future as the Apollyon. She has battled with her love for Aiden and the knowledge that they are not supposed to be together. She has battled with the loss of her parents. It is in this book that she truly matures into a beautiful, strong, driven young woman. Alex trains in order to p</span>
  <span id="freeText14370330969681367636" style="display:none"> <b>"It's time!"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422854941i/13554782.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sentinel is the fifth and final book of the Covenant series. Everything that has transpired in the past four books has been leading to this moment! Sentinel did not disappoint.<br><br>Alex has been battling her future as the Apollyon. She has battled with her love for Aiden and the knowledge that they are not supposed to be together. She has battled with the loss of her parents. It is in this book that she truly matures into a beautiful, strong, driven young woman. Alex trains in order to prepare herself for the fight that will save the world.<br><br>Finally, she and Aiden have decided not to leave their love in the closet anymore. It was so freeing for them to just be together. Ms. Armentrout knows how to write a good love story. We have watched these two come together only to be forced apart. To see them side by side was truly beautiful! <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422854941i/13554783._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Aiden and Alex aren't the only ones that receive resolution in this final book. Seth is able to come through for Alex. He has been her friend. He has been her enemy. In his own way, he loves Alex. He knows he cannot have her. He knows he cannot be the Apollyon. No matter what my thoughts have been of Seth, he truly came through for Alex in the end.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422854941i/13554784._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is not much I can say with out ruining this story for you. What I will say is that the Covenant series is by far one of the best series I have ever read. The primary and secondary characters are well developed and there are many layers to the plot. These books are full of action, suspense, passion, drama, and everything in between. I am truly saddened to be finished with this series. I know that I will be rereading them again soon.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1422855387i/13554824._SY540_.jpg" width="" height="" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="14370330969681367636" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1369694319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7301998171999539256">This has been one of the most amazing journeys I've engaged in my life. This 5 covenant books have rocked my world. Once again JLA leaves me with my mouth hanging wide open!<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455218054ra/18075250.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><b>(keep in mind that this is a review of the complete series.)</b><br/><br/>For the last week this book did numerous things to me:<br/><b>1. Happy</b><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455514550ra/18110886.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I love how quick Alex was to answer. I loved her stubbornness, I loved how hardheaded she was and how she didn't take shit from anyone. How all of her actions came from the heart and not from her head.<br/><br/><b>2.It</b></span>
  <span id="freeText7301998171999539256" style="display:none">This has been one of the most amazing journeys I've engaged in my life. This 5 covenant books have rocked my world. Once again JLA leaves me with my mouth hanging wide open!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455218054ra/18075250.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>(keep in mind that this is a review of the complete series.)</b><br><br>For the last week this book did numerous things to me:<br><b>1. Happy</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455514550ra/18110886.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I love how quick Alex was to answer. I loved her stubbornness, I loved how hardheaded she was and how she didn't take shit from anyone. How all of her actions came from the heart and not from her head.<br><br><b>2.It kept me intrigued</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455218054ra/18075251.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>The way the story itself developed was amazing. Alex and Aiden, and all of her friends were all strong characters. I mean sure, they all had their flaws, but even Lea was incredibly brave. Marcus and Seth were just amazing characters. And even though we lost Seth for a couple of books there, he still managed to keep a part of our hearts.<br><br><b>3.Angry</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1452442484ra/17694622.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I think this gif is really appropriate for how I felt most of the time reading this book. Specially with the gods. There's a statement that Alex makes in this book, where she tell Apollo that the battle that they were fighting, wasn't their battle but the gods, and yet they've all dumped their issues into the human world. Well I was pretty pissed with everyone. I am not sure I like the ending of this book very much--don't get me wrong--I am happy for them, but it was weird ending considering all the other alternatives that this book could've ended, but oh well. I was angry, as well, with Alex believe or not, sometimes she could get under my skin, and Seth, well he is another story.<br><br><b>4.Sad</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1455218054ra/18075252.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So many deaths, OH MY GODS, so many unnecessary deaths. Everything was so devastating, and in the end of this book, I just couldn't take anymore. I broke down and cried for all of those characters who didn't made it through, I even cried for those who I thought didn't make it, but that if I kept reading I might have save some tears. But still, it was heart crushing.<br><br>But I'm really happy that I've ended this incredible and amazing journey with Alex and Aiden, and all of their friends, and even enemies. This is a series that would always be a part of my heart.</span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('oZXAxOoeJi8IiQ9+RNt09gg4Qxrl30WEeHlHSbbeqwqbs6kWUUDvR6+iux+zLn4p3mek0itSy+MjBwH4e51ZkA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2bRPvkRAzNy5T0mjInBcJ4/xBrg61o234E1h0pZVnfDjkiZs/x4FtB5k/cLVhVb4Wa7hcPRbA9C7MydjWxZvag==')})
  }

All the rumors yo</span>
  <span id="freeText12509967403922046863" style="display:none">Hey Guys! Please note: I don't send out ARCs for review. If you're interested in reviewing a book of mine before release date, please contact the appropriate publisher. I also do NOT check my Goodreads email.<br /><br />To email me, please use the below addy. <br />jenniferlarmentrout@live.com<br /><br /># 1 New York Times and # 1 International Bestselling author Jennifer lives in Charles Town, West Virginia. All the rumors you’ve heard about her state aren’t true. When she’s not hard at work writing. she spends her time reading, watching really bad zombie movies, pretending to write, hanging out with her husband and her Jack Russell Loki. In early 2015, Jennifer was diagnosed with retinitis pigmentosa, a group of rare genetic disorders that involve a breakdown and death of cells in the retina, eventually resulting in loss of vision, among other complications. Due to this diagnosis, educating people on the varying degrees of blindness has become of passion of hers, right alongside writing, which she plans to do as long as she can. <br /><br />Her dreams of becoming an author started in algebra class, where she spent most of her time writing short stories….which explains her dismal grades in math. Jennifer writes young adult paranormal, science fiction, fantasy, and contemporary romance. She is published with Tor, HarperCollins Avon and William Morrow, Entangled Teen and Brazen, Disney/Hyperion and Harlequin Teen. Her Wicked Series has been optioned by PassionFlix. Jennifer has won numerous awards, including the 2013 Reviewers Choice Award for Wait for You, the 2015 Editor’s Pick for Fall With Me, and the 2014/2015 Moerser-Jugendbuch- Jury award for Obsidian. Her young adult romantic suspense novel DON’T LOOK BACK was a 2014 nominated Best in Young Adult Fiction by YALSA. Her adult romantic suspense novel TILL DEATH was a Amazon Editor’s Pick and iBook Book of the Month. Her young adult contemporary THE PROBLEM WITH FOREVER is a 2017 RITA Award Winner in Young Adult Fiction. She also writes Adult and New Adult contemporary and paranormal romance under the name J. Lynn. She is published by Entangled Brazen and HarperCollins.<br /><br />She is the owner of ApollyCon and The Origin Event, the successful annual events that features over hundred bestselling authors in Young Adult, New Adult, and Adult Fiction, panels, parties, and more.</span>
